</li></ul>
</dt></dl>
<ol><li>Communion (G major, 1864)
</li><li>Marche religieuse (F major, 1864, on a motive of one of Handel's choruses)

</li></ol>

</li></ul>

</li></ul>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li>Collection as a whole published by <a href="/wiki/Schott" title="Schott">Schott</a> in 1892 (<span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://anno.onb.ac.at/cgi-content/anno-buch?apm=0&amp;aid=1000001&amp;bd=0001892&amp;teil=0203&amp;seite=00000149&amp;zoom=1">Hofmeister's <i>Monatsbericht</i> (1892), p.149</a></span>). This is definitely not the earliest publication date of most if any of the works in the collection and may not even be the earliest publication date of the collection.
</li></ul>
